<t>CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Food (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2), quantity INT);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Beverage (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), brand VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Ingredient (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);

<t>CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Food (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), category VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2), quantity INT);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Beverage (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(255), brand VARCHAR(255), price DECIMAL(10, 2);
